1	# Proof outline — verified hex0 (the refinement methodology)
2	
3	This documents *how* the hex0 verification is structured, so the proof can be
4	audited, maintained, and **re-implemented in another proof assistant** (the Coq
5	port follows this outline verbatim). Read with `STATUS.md` (state), `TCB.md`
6	(trust boundary), `HEX0.md` (the language).
7	
8	## 1. The verification tower
9	
10	```
11	   HEX0.md BNF  ⟺  decodeS / coreSpec  ⟸  RV64I model running the real bytes
12	   (grammar)        (functional spec)       (binary, byte-for-byte)
13	   └─ Grammar.lean ─┘└──────────── Refine.lean (core_refines) ───────────┘
14	```
15	
16	Two independent proofs meet at the functional spec:
17	
18	- **`Grammar.lean`** — the published BNF (`HEX0.md`) `⟺` the spec `decodeS`
19	  (sound + complete; the grammar is total and deterministic). Anchors "is the
20	  spec the language we documented?".
21	- **`Refine.lean`** — `core_refines`: for **all** inputs, the real `core` bytes
22	  executed on the RV64I model compute exactly `coreSpec`. Anchors "do the bytes
23	  that run implement the spec?".
24	
25	Everything below is the structure of `Refine.lean` (the hard half), then the
26	`Grammar.lean` layer, then the Coq port plan.
27	
28	## 2. Objects
29	
30	- **Model** (`Rv64i`): `State = (reg, pc, mem)`, a pure `step : State → State`
31	  over the 12 instruction forms `core` uses (`addi add or slli lbu sb beq blt
32	  bge bgeu jal jalr`), `runFuel`/`runUntil` to iterate. No CSRs, traps,
33	  privilege, or stack (`core` is a leaf function — see TCB / the input contract).
34	- **Spec** (`Spec`): `decodeS : St → List Nat → (List Nat × Status)`, a two-state
35	  (`High`/`Low`) functional decoder; `coreSpec` wraps it with the output-capacity
36	  (`OutputShort`) bound.
37	- **Harness**: `initOn`/`mkInit` (the entry state: code+input loaded, `a0..a3`
38	  set, `ra=0`), `observe`/`runOn` (run and read back `a0`,`a1`, output region).
39	
40	## 3. The theorem and its preconditions
41	
42	```
43	core_refines : ∀ inp cap, WellFormed inp cap →
44	                 ∃ fuel, observe inp cap fuel = coreSpec inp cap
45	```
46	`WellFormed inp cap` (the input contract):
47	- `in_fits  : inputAddr + |inp| ≤ outAddr`   — input/output regions disjoint.
48	- `out_fits : outAddr + cap < 2^64`           — output region fits, no wraparound.
49	- `bytes_ok : ∀ b ∈ inp, b < 256`             — inputs are bytes.
50	
51	Implicit (in `initOn`): fixed memory layout (code abuts input: `coreAddr+324 =
52	inputAddr`), `ra=0` with "return = halt (pc→0)", no stack used. (See TCB.)
53	
54	## 4. Methodology — refinement by loop invariant + induction (4 steps)
55	
56	1. **Base case** (`core_eof`): from the loop head with input exhausted, the
57	   machine runs `bgeu(taken);li a0,0;mv a1,t1;ret`, halting `Ok` with output
58	   preserved.
59	2. **Loop-state model** (`LoopInv inp cap s rest emitted`): a 16-field invariant
60	   relating a mid-execution state to a *partial* run of `decodeS` — `rest` is the
61	   unconsumed input suffix, `emitted` the bytes written, with the telescoping
62	   field `spec_link : decodeS High inp = (emitted ++ (decodeS High rest).1, …)`,
63	   plus register/memory facts and the static region bounds (`in_fits`,`out_lt`).
64	3. **Token decomposition**:
65	   - *spec side* (`decodeS_spacing/byte/comment_skip`): one `decodeS` step per
66	     token class.
67	   - *machine side* (`loop_iteration`): from a non-empty `rest`, the machine
68	     either returns to the loop head with a strictly shorter `rest` and `LoopInv`
69	     preserved, or halts in a `coreSpec`-correct error state. A **dispatch on the
70	     head char's class** (see §6).
71	4. **Induction** (`loop_correct`): structural induction on a fuel bound on
72	   `|rest|`; base = `core_eof`, step = `loop_iteration`, chained by `runFuel_add`,
73	   telescoped by `spec_link`. Then assemble with the **prologue**
74	   (`init_loopinv`) and the **`observe↔coreSpec` conversion**.
75	
76	## 5. The lemma DAG (depe

17	- **BUILD GOTCHA (cost real time):** `lake build`'s default target only built
18	  what `lean/Hex0.lean` imports. That root did NOT import `Refine`, so
19	  `lake build` reported success *without ever type-checking `Refine.lean`* (and
20	  served a stale `.olean`). Fixed: `Hex0.lean` now imports `Refine`/`Image`/
21	  `Harness`/`Certify`. **To validate `Refine` directly without cache, use
22	  `lake env lean Hex0/Refine.lean`** (errors print top-down; exit 0 = clean).
23	  Also note `set`/`List.getD_eq_getElem` are Mathlib/Batteries-only — unavailable
24	  here; use `let x := e; have h : x = e := rfl; rw [← h] at <hyp>` and
25	  `(List.getElem_eq_getD 0)` instead.
26	- The remaining frontier is now **task #7** (ISA cross-check) and the single
27	  Coq `Refine.v` hole `loop_iteration` (the per-token dispatch; `core_refines`
28	  itself is proved modulo it).
29	
30	## Environment gotchas (these cost real time — don't rediscover)
31	
32	- **Lean is 4.30.0 via elan; there is NO Mathlib.** Consequences:
33	  - **Banned tactics/lemmas**: `norm_num`, `ring`/`ring_nf`, `set ... with`,
34	    `omega` does NOT evaluate `2^64` reliably as a bound unless the other facts
35	    pin it (it's usually fine, but for `a < 2^64` from `a < small` it works).
36	    `le_refl` unqualified is absent → use `Nat.le_refl`.
37	  - **Use instead**: `decide` (for closed nat/BitVec goals incl. `2 < 2^64`),
38	    `omega` (linear nat), `simp`, `Nat.le_refl`, `List.ext_getElem`.
39	  - `set x := e with h` → replace with `let x := e` + `have h : x = e := rfl` +
40	    `rw [← h] at <hyps mentioning e>`.
41	- **`set_option maxRecDepth 4000 in` MUST come BEFORE the doc comment**, not
42	  between the doc comment and the `theorem`. `/-- … -/ set_option … in theorem`
43	  is a parse error ("unexpected token set_option").
44	- **`decide` chokes on free variables.** `(by decide)` proving e.g.
45	  `BitVec.ofNat 64 (coreAddr + off) ≠ 0` fails when `off` is symbolic. Use
46	  `ofNat_ne` (proved) with explicit bound proofs, or reduce to a closed term
47	  first (`simp only [Image.coreAddr]; omega`).
48	- `decide` needs `maxRecDepth ~4000` whenever it evaluates `Image.coreBytes.length`
49	  (a 324-element list) or 64-bit BitVec arithmetic with ~2³¹ addresses.
50	- **`by` inside an anonymous constructor `⟨…⟩` is greedy** — it swallows the
51	  following tuple elements. Always parenthesize: `⟨(by decide), …⟩`.
52	- `simp` will collapse `x = x` to `True`; then provide `trivial`, not `rfl`.
53	- **`native_decide` works but adds the Lean compiler to the TCB** — used only in
54	  `lean/Hex0/Certify.lean` (the finite cert). Coq's `Certify.v` is kernel-checked
55	  via `vm_compute` (smaller TCB) — keep that contrast.
56	- **`Harness.loadBytes` was rewritten recursively** (not `foldl`) so it's provable
57	  by induction; semantics identical, certs still pass.
58	- Namespace clash: inside `namespace Hex0.Refine` with `open Rv64i`, plain
59	  `decode` = `Rv64i.decode`; the spec's is `Hex0.decode`. **Qualify `Hex0.…`**
60	  for spec stuff (`Hex0.decodeS`, `Hex0.nibble`, `Hex0.coreS

399	(* Base case: input exhausted -> halts Ok with output preserved. (Uses core_eof;
400	   the readMem/coreSpec packaging is the remaining detail -- Admitted for now.) *)
401	Theorem eof_result : forall inp cap emitted s,
402	  LoopInv inp cap s [] emitted -> Result (runUntil 0 4 s) inp cap.
403	Proof.
404	  intros inp cap emitted s HI.
405	  destruct HI as [Hpc Hcode Ha0 Ha1 Ha2 Ha3 Hra Hinmem Hinlt Hbytes Hinfits Houtlt
406	                  Hidx Hsuf Houtidx Hemitle Houtmem Hspec].
407	  assert (h5 : rget s 5 = Z.of_nat (length inp)) by (rewrite Hidx; simpl length; lia).
408	  assert (hE : 0 <= Z.of_nat (length emitted) < 2 ^ 64) by (unfold outAddr in Houtlt; lia).
409	  destruct (core_eof s (Z.of_nat (length inp)) (Z.of_nat (length emitted))
410	              Hcode Hpc h5 Ha1 Houtidx Hra hE) as [Hp [H10 [H11 Hmem]]].
411	  (* coreSpec computes to (0, emitted, length emitted) *)
412	  assert (Hdec : Spec.decode (zin inp) = (emitted, Ok)).
413	  { unfold Spec.decode. rewrite Hspec. change (zin []) with (@nil nat).
414	    rewrite decodeS_nil. simpl. rewrite app_nil_r. reflexivity. }
415	  assert (Hcs : coreSpec (zin inp) (Z.to_nat cap) = (0%nat, emitted, length emitted)).
416	  { unfold coreSpec. rewrite Hdec.
417	    destruct (Z.to_nat cap <? length emitted)%nat eqn:Ecap.
418	    - apply Nat.ltb_lt in Ecap. lia.
419	    - reflexivity. }
420	  unfold Result. rewrite Hcs. repeat split.
421	  - exact Hp.
422	  - rewrite H10. reflexivity.
423	  - rewrite H11. reflexivity.
424	  - rewrite Hmem. apply readMem_eq. intros j Hj. exact (Houtmem j Hj).
425	Qed.
426	
427	(** ** Reusable machine-stepping blocks (mirror of lean/Hex0/Refine.lean's
428	    "reusable blocks").  Ported bottom-up; each is consumed by the per-token
429	    [loop_*] cases that build [loop_iteration]. *)
430	
431	(* [li t3,K; beq t2,t3,_] where t2 = c <> K: runs as 2 steps, the beq falling
432	   through (not taken) to off+8.  Clobbers only t3 (=x28) and pc.  Mirror of the
433	   Lean [li_beq_ne].  (t2 = x7, t3 = x28.) *)
434	Lemma li_beq_ne s off K c imm :
435	  CodeLoaded s -> 0 <= off -> off + 4 + 3 < Z.of_nat (length coreBytes) ->
436	  s.(pc) = coreAddr + off ->
437	  rget s 7 = c ->
438	  decode (wordAt off) = Iaddi 28 0 K ->
439	  decode (wordAt (off + 4)) = Ibeq 7 28 imm ->
440	  0 <= K < 2 ^ 64 ->
441	  c <> K ->
442	  runUntil 0 2 s = setPc (rset s 28 K) (coreAddr + (off + 8)).
443	Proof.
444	  intros hc ho hb hpc h7 hli hbeq hK hne.
445	  rewrite coreBytes_len in hb.
446	  assert (ho1 : off + 3 < Z.of_nat (length coreBytes)) by (rewrite coreBytes_len; lia).
447	  assert (hu1 : step s = setPc (rset s 28 K) (coreAddr + (off + 4))).
448	  { rewrite (step_addi s off 28 0 K hc ho ho1 hpc hli), rget_zero,
449	      (wadd_id 0 K ltac:(lia)), Z.add_0_l, hpc,
450	      (wadd_id (coreAddr + off) 4 ltac:(unfold coreAddr; lia)).
451	    f_equal. lia. }
452	  set (s1 := setPc (rset s 28 K) (coreAddr + (off + 4))) in *.
453	  assert (hc1 : CodeLoaded s1)
454	    by (apply (CodeLoaded_eqmem s); [unfold s1; rewrite setPc_mem, rset_mem; reflexivity| exact hc]).
455	  assert (hpc1 : s1.(pc) = coreAddr + (off + 4)) by reflexivity.
456	  assert (h7s1 : rget s1 7 = c) by (unfold s1; rewrite setPc_rget; exact h7).
457	  assert (h28s1 : rget s1 28 = K) by (unfold s1; rewrite setPc_rget; reflexivity).
458	  assert (hu2 : step s1 = setPc s1 (coreAddr + (off + 8))).
459	  { rewrite (step_beq s1 (off + 4) 7 28 imm hc1 ltac:(lia)
460	              ltac:(rewrite coreBytes_len; lia) hpc1 hbeq), h7s1, h28s1.
461	    replace (c =? K) with false by (symmetry; apply Z.eqb_neq; exact hne).
462	    rewrite hpc1, (wadd_id (coreAddr + (off + 4)) 4 ltac:(unfold coreAddr; lia)).
463	    f_equal. lia. }
464	  assert (hp0 : s.(pc) <> 0) by (rewrite hpc; unfold coreAddr; lia).
465	  assert (hp1 : s1.(pc) <> 0) by (rewrite hpc1; unfold coreAddr; lia).
466	  rewrite (runUntil_S 1 s hp0), hu1, (runUntil_S 0 s1 hp1), hu2.
467	  unfold s1. reflexivity.
468	Qed.
469	
470	(* [li t3,K; beq t2,t3,_] w
… [truncated 3345 chars]

479	theorem loop_prefix (inp : List Nat) (cap : Nat) (c : Nat) (rest' emitted : List Nat)
480	    (s : State) (inv : LoopInv inp cap s (c :: rest') emitted) :
481	    ∃ s4, runFuel 0 4 s = s4 ∧

### 👤 **User**

```
1	(** * General refinement (T1) in Coq -- mirror of lean/Hex0/Refine.lean.
2	
3	    Proof-grade theorem: for ALL inputs, the real `core` computes `coreSpec`.
4	    No vm_compute on the general statement -- it is genuine induction.
5	
6	    STATUS: `core_refines` is PROVED modulo the single per-token dispatch lemma
7	    `loop_iteration` (the only `Admitted`).  Everything that assembles it is
8	    kernel-checked, mirroring `lean/Hex0/Refine.lean` §5:
9	      - `fetch_code` + all 12 `step_*` lemmas + state/storeByte projections
10	        (`decode (wordAt off)` reduces under `vm_compute` at concrete offsets, so
11	        the step lemmas apply exactly as in Lean);
12	      - arithmetic toolkit: `wrap_small`, `wadd_id`, `toS_small`, `sltb_small`;
13	      - `runUntil` composition: `runUntil_halt`, `runUntil_one`, `runUntil_S`,
14	        `runUntil_add`, `runUntil_stab` (large-fuel halt absorption);
15	      - spec-side token decomposition: `decodeS_spacing`/`byte`/`comment`;
16	      - `core_eof` -- the EOF base case (4-step run to a correct halt);
17	      - `LoopInv` (the 18-field invariant) + `eof_result`;
18	      - `loop_correct` -- the induction (fuel bound `50*|rest| + 4`);
19	      - `init_loopinv` -- the prologue (2-step run to the loop head);
20	      - `core_refines` -- prologue + induction + `runOn<->coreSpec` conversion.
21	    Remaining frontier (`Admitted`, line ~425): `loop_iteration` -- the per-token
22	    dispatch (spacing/byte/comment + the four halting error classes), the large
23	    mechanical tail (~2500 Lean lines).  `Print Assumptions core_refines` =>
24	    `loop_iteration` + `functional_extensionality_dep` (a standard, consistent
25	    axiom, used for `mem : Z -> Z` state equality -- cf. Lean's propext/choice).
26	    Two Coq-specific notes vs Lean (see PROOF.md §8): (1) `runOn` uses a *fixed*
27	    fuel (100000), so the assembly bounds the step count (Lean used ∃fuel) and
28	    absorbs the slack via `runUntil_stab` -- note `lia` cannot reason about the
29	    nat literal `100000` (it is `Nat.of_num_uint`), so the bound `F <= 100000`
30	    is proved through `Z` (`Nat2Z.inj_le` + `vm_compute (Z.of_nat 100000)`);
31	    (2) the model's bytes are `Z` but the spec is on `nat`, so `LoopInv`/dispatch
32	    carry `Z.of_nat`/`Z.to_nat` (`zin`) conversions. *)
33	
34	From Coq Require Import ZArith List Lia Bool.
35	From Equations Require Import Equations.
36	From Hex0Coq Require Import Spec Rv64i Image Harness.
37	Import ListNotations.
38	Local Open Scope Z_scope.
39	
40	(** ** Per-step reduction primitive (PROVED).
41	    `core`'s first instruction `li t0,0` = `addi x5,x0,0`, bytes 93 02 00 00,
42	    word 0x293 = 659. One [step] computes its effect; data stays symbolic. *)
43	Theorem step_li_t0 : forall s,
44	  s.(mem) s.(pc) = 147 ->
45	  s.(mem) (s.(pc) + 1) = 2 ->
46	  s.(mem) (s.(pc) + 2) = 0 ->
47	  s.(mem) (s.(pc) + 3) = 0 ->
48	  s.(pc) = 2147483784 ->
49	  (step s).(pc) = 2147483788 /\ rget (step s) 5 = 0.
50	Proof.
51	  intros s h0 h1 h2 h3 hpc.
52	  unfold step, fetch32.
53	  rewrite h0, h1, h2, h3.
54	  (* fetched word is now the closed value 659; decode + effect compute *)
55	  change (147 + 2 * 256 + 0 * 65536 + 0 * 16777216) with 659.
56	  rewrite hpc. cbn. split; reflexivity.
57	Qed.
58	
59	(** ** Engine: fetch at a code offset + per-instruction step lemmas.

61	    decode of a closed word reduces under [cbn]/[vm_compute] at call sites. *)

63	Definition nthb (i : Z) : Z := nth (Z.to_nat i) coreBytes 0.
64	
65	Definition wordAt (off : Z) : Z :=
66	  nthb off + nthb (off + 1) * 256 + nthb (off + 2) * 65536 + nthb (off + 3) * 16777216.

200	(** ** Arithmetic toolkit (mirror of ult_ofNat/slt_ofNat/ofNat_ne/setWidth8). *)
201	
202	Lemma wrap_small z : 0 <= z < 2 ^ 64 -> wrap z = z.
203	Proof. unfold wrap, w64. apply Z.mod_small. Qed.
204	
205	(* address arithmetic with no 64-bit wraparound *)
206	Lemma wadd_id a b : 0 <= a + b < 2 ^ 64 -> wadd a b = a + b.
207	Proof. unfold wadd. apply wrap_small. Qed.
208	
209	Lemma toS_small x : 0 <= x < 2 ^ 63 -> toS x = x.
210	Proof. unfold toS. intros h. destruct (x >=? 2 ^ 63) eqn:E; [lia | reflexivity]. Qed.
211	
212	(* signed compare = unsigned compare on small (< 2^63) values *)
213	Lemma sltb_small a b : 0 <= a < 2 ^ 63 -> 0 <= b < 2 ^ 63 -> sltb a b = (a <? b).
214	Proof. intros ha hb. unfold sltb. rewrite (toS_small a ha), (toS_small b hb). reflexivity. Qed.
215	
216	(** ** runUntil (= Lean runFuel) composition. *)
217	
218	Lemma runUntil_halt n s : s.(pc) = 0 -> runUntil 0 n s = s.
219	Proof. intros h. destruct n; [reflexivity|]. simpl. rewrite h, Z.eqb_refl. reflexivity. Qed.
220	
221	Lemma runUntil_one s : s.(pc) <> 0 -> runUntil 0 1 s = step s.
222	Proof.
223	  intros h. simpl. destruct (s.(pc) =? 0) eqn:E; [apply Z.eqb_eq in E; lia | reflexivity].
224	Qed.
225	
226	Lemma runUntil_S n s : s.(pc) <> 0 -> runUntil 0 (S n) s = runUntil 0 n (step s).
227	Proof.
228	  intros h. simpl. destruct (s.(pc) =? 0) eqn:E; [apply Z.eqb_eq in E; lia | reflexivity].
229	Qed.
230	
231	Lemma runUntil_add a b s : runUntil 0 (a + b) s = runUntil 0 b (runUntil 0 a s).
232	Proof.
233	  revert b s. induction a as [|k ih]; intros b s; simpl; [reflexivity|].
234	  destruct (s.(pc) =? 0) eqn:E.
235	  - apply Z.eqb_eq in E. now rewrite (runUntil_halt b s E).
236	  - apply ih.
237	Qed.
238	
239	(* Once the machine has halted by fuel [f], any larger fuel [g] gives the same
240	   state.  Used to absorb the fixed 100000-fuel run in [runOn] into the
241	   step-count bound the loop actually needs (avoids nat-subtraction lia, which
242	   chokes on the [Nat.of_num_uint 100000] literal). *)
243	Lemma runUntil_stab f s : (runUntil 0 f s).(pc) = 0 ->
244	  forall g, (f <= g)%nat -> runUntil 0 g s = runUntil 0 f s.
245	Proof.
246	  intros Hhalt g Hle. induction Hle as [|g Hle IH].
247	  - reflexivity.
248	  - rewrite <- Nat.add_1_r, (runUntil_add g 1 s), IH.
249	    exact (runUntil_halt 1 (runUntil 0 f s) Hhalt).
250	Qed.
251	
252	(** ** Spec-side token decomposition (mirror of decodeS_spacing/byte/comment). *)
253	
254	Lemma decodeS_spacing c rest : isComment c = false -> isSpace c = true ->
255	  decodeS High (c :: rest) = decodeS High rest.
256	Proof. intros hc hs. simp decodeS. rewrite hc, hs. reflexivity. Qed.
257	
258	Lemma decodeS_byte chi clo rest hi lo :
259	  isComment chi = false -> isSpace chi = false -> nibble chi = Some hi ->
260	  isLowStop clo = false -> nibble clo = Some lo ->
261	  decodeS High (chi :: clo :: rest) =
262	    ((hi * 16 + lo)%nat :: fst (decodeS High rest), snd (decodeS High rest)).
263	Proof.
264	  intros hc hs hh hlc hl. simp decodeS. rewrite hc, hs, hh. simp decodeS. rewrite hlc, hl.
265	  destruct (decodeS High rest) as [out st]. reflexivity.
266	Qed.
267	
268	Lemma decodeS_comment c rest : isComment c = true ->
269	  decodeS High (c :: rest) = decodeS High (skipComment rest).
270	Proof. intros hc. simp decodeS. rewrite hc. reflexivity. Qed.
271	
272	(** ** EOF base case (mirror of core_eof). *)
273	
274	Lemma coreBytes_len : Z.of_nat (length coreBytes) = 324. Proof. reflexivity. Qed.
275	Lemma coreAddr_pos k : 0 <= k -> coreAddr + k <> 0. Proof. unfold coreAddr; lia. Qed.
276	Lemma CodeLoaded_eqmem s t : t.(mem) = s.(mem) -> CodeLoaded s -> CodeLoaded t.
277	Proof. intros hm hcs i Hi. rewrite hm. apply hcs; exact Hi. Qed.

Refine.v:643:  runOn inp cap = specOn (zin inp) (Z.to_nat cap).
=== Spec key ===
Definition isLowStop (c:nat) : bool := isSpace c || isComment c.

(* nibble value 0..15, or None if c is not an uppercase hex digit. *)
Definition nibble (c:nat) : option nat :=
  if (48 <=? c) && (c <=? 57) then Some (c - 48)        (* '0'..'9' *)
  else if (65 <=? c) && (c <=? 70) then Some (c - 55)   (* 'A'..'F' -> 10..15 *)
  else None.

(* Terminal status of a decode (capacity-independent). *)
Inductive Status := Ok | Split | Trailing | Unknown.

(* Skip a comment body: drop characters up to and including the first '\n'.
   (In core.s the '\n' is left for the main loop and skipped there as spacing;
   the net effect is the same -- continue at the character after the newline.) *)
Fixpoint skipComment (l:list nat) : list nat :=
  match l with
  | [] => []
  | c :: rest => if c =? c_nl then rest else skipComment rest
  end.

Lemma skipComment_len : forall l, length (skipComment l) <= length l.
Proof.
  induction l as [|c rest IH]; simpl; [lia|].
  destruct (c =? c_nl); simpl; lia.
Qed.

(* Decoder state. *)
Inductive St := High | Low (hi:nat).

Equations? decodeS (s:St) (l:list nat) : (list nat * Status) by wf (length l) lt :=
  decodeS High [] := ([], Ok);
  decodeS (Low _) [] := ([], Trailing);
  decodeS High (c :: rest) :=
    if isComment c then decodeS High (skipComment rest)
    else if isSpace c then decodeS High rest
    else match nibble c with
         | None => ([], Unknown)
         | Some hi => decodeS (Low hi) rest
         end;
  decodeS (Low hi) (c :: rest) :=
    if isLowStop c then ([], Split)
    else match nibble c with
         | None => ([], Unknown)
         | Some lo => let '(out, st) := decodeS High rest in
                      (hi * 16 + lo :: out, st)
         end.
Proof.
  all: simpl in *; try lia.
  all: match goal with
       | [ |- context[length (skipComment ?l)] ] =>
           pose proof (skipComment_len l); lia
       end.
Qed.

Definition decode (l:list nat) : (list nat * Status) := decodeS High l.

(* Numeric status codes, matching the Error enum in hex0.c / core.s. *)
Definition statusCode (s:Status) : nat :=
  match s with Ok => 0 | Split => 3 | Trailing => 4 | Unknown => 5 end.

(* Behaviour of the bounded machine `core` with output capacity [cap]:
   capacity is checked just before each store, so if the decode would emit
   more than [cap] bytes, the machine stops with OutputShort (code 2) having
   written exactly the first [cap] bytes. Returns (status, output, out_len). *)
Definition coreSpec (input:list nat) (cap:nat) : (nat * list nat * nat) :=
  let '(bs, st) := decode input in
  if cap <? length bs
  then (2, firstn cap bs, cap)
  else (statusCode st, bs, length bs).
```

### 👤 **User**

**↩︎ tool result**
```
skipn_skipn
     : forall (A : Type) (x y : nat) (l : list A),
       skipn x (skipn y l) = skipn (x + y) l
firstn_skipn
     : forall (A : Type) (n : nat) (l : list A), firstn n l ++ skipn n l = l
in_or_app
     : forall (A : Type) (l m : list A) (a : A),
       In a l \/ In a m -> In a (l ++ m)
orb_true_iff
     : forall b1 b2 : bool, b1 || b2 = true <-> b1 = true \/ b2 = true
Z2Nat.id
     : forall n : Z, (0 <= n)%Z -> Z.of_nat (Z.to_nat n) = n
```

theorem error_result (s : State) (inp : List Nat) (cap : Nat) (emitted : List Nat)
    (st : Hex0.Status) (hp : s.pc = 0)
    (ha0 : s.rget 10 = BitVec.ofNat 64 (Hex0.statusCode st))
    (ha1 : s.rget 11 = BitVec.ofNat 64 emitted.length)
    (hmem : ∀ j, j < emitted.length →
      s.mem (BitVec.ofNat 64 (Image.outAddr + j)) = BitVec.ofNat 8 (emitted.getD j 0))
    (hdec : Hex0.decode inp = (emitted, st)) (hle : emitted.length ≤ cap) :
    Result s inp cap := by
  have hcs : Hex0.coreSpec inp cap = (Hex0.statusCode st, emitted, emitted.length) := by
    simp only [Hex0.coreSpec, hdec]; rw [if_neg (Nat.not_lt.mpr hle)]
  refine ⟨hp, ?_, ?_, ?_⟩
  · rw [ha0, hcs]
  · rw [ha1, hcs]
  · intro j hj; rw [hcs] at hj ⊢; exact hmem j hj
```

Z.add_lor_land: forall x y : Z, Z.lor x y + Z.land x y = x + y
Z.sub_2lor_lxor: forall x y : Z, 2 * Z.lor x y - Z.lxor x y = x + y
Z.addcarryeqn:
  forall (x y : Z) (c0 : bool),
  let z := x + y + Z.b2z c0 in
  let c := Z.lxor z (Z.lxor x y) in
  Z.shiftr c 1 = Z.lor (Z.land x y) (Z.land c (Z.lxor x y))
Z.add_carry_bits:
  forall (a b : Z) (c0 : bool),
  exists c : Z,
    a + b + Z.b2z c0 = Z.lxor (Z.lxor a b) c /\
    c / 2 = Z.lor (Z.land a b) (Z.land c (Z.lor a b)) /\ Z.testbit c 0 = c0
Z.add_carry_bits_aux:
  forall n : Z,
  0 <= n ->
  forall (a b : Z) (c0 : bool),
  - 2 ^ n <= a < 2 ^ n ->
  - 2 ^ n <= b < 2 ^ n ->
  exists c : Z,
    a + b + Z.b2z c0 = Z.lxor (Z.lxor a b) c /\
    c / 2 = Z.lor (Z.land a b) (Z.land c (Z.lor a b)) /\ Z.testbit c 0 = c0
```

### 👤 **User**

**↩︎ tool result**
```
Theorem loop_correct : forall inp cap n rest emitted s,
  (length rest <= n)%nat -> LoopInv inp cap s rest emitted ->
  Result (runUntil 0 (50 * length rest + 4) s) inp cap.
Proof.
  intros inp cap n. induction n as [|n IH]; intros rest emitted s hn hinv.
  - assert (rest = []) by (destruct rest; [reflexivity| simpl in hn; lia]).
    subst rest. exact (eof_result inp cap emitted s hinv).
  - destruct rest as [|c rest''] eqn:Er.
    + exact (eof_result inp cap emitted s hinv).
    + destruct (loop_iteration inp cap (c :: rest'') emitted s ltac:(discriminate) hinv)
        as [k [ [rest' [emitted' [Hlt [Hkb Hinv']]]] | [Hkb Hres] ]].
      * (* continue: k <= 50*(|rest|-|rest'|) chars consumed *)
        set (A := (50 * length (c :: rest'') + 4)%nat).
        assert (HkA : (k <= A)%nat) by (unfold A; lia).
        replace A with (k + (A - k))%nat by lia. rewrite runUntil_add.
        assert (HBle : (50 * length rest' + 4 <= A - k)%nat) by (unfold A; simpl length in *; lia).
        replace (A - k)%nat with ((50 * length rest' + 4) + ((A - k) - (50 * length rest' + 4)))%nat by lia.
        rewrite runUntil_add.
        assert (HIH : Result (runUntil 0 (50 * length rest' + 4) (runUntil 0 k s)) inp cap)
          by (apply (IH rest' emitted'); [simpl length in *; lia | exact Hinv']).
        rewrite (runUntil_halt _ _ (Result_pc _ _ _ HIH)). exact HIH.
      * (* halt *)
        set (A := (50 * length (c :: rest'') + 4)%nat).
        assert (HkA : (k <= A)%nat) by (unfold A; lia).
        replace A with (k + (A - k))%nat by lia. rewrite runUntil_add.
        rewrite (runUntil_halt _ _ (Result_pc _ _ _ Hres)). exact Hres.
Qed.
```

Lemma loop_comment inp cap c rest' emitted s :
  isComment (Z.to_nat c) = true ->
  LoopInv inp cap s (c :: rest') emitted ->
  exists k, (exists rest'' emitted', (length rest'' < length (c :: rest'))%nat /\
              LoopInv inp cap (runUntil 0 k s) rest'' emitted')
         \/ Result (runUntil 0 k s) inp cap.
Proof.
  intros hcm inv. pose proof inv as inv0.
  destruct (loopinv_head inp cap c rest' emitted s inv) as [Hin Hc].
  destruct (loop_prefix inp cap c rest' emitted s inv) as [hpc4 [ht2 [ht0 [hmem4 [hcode4 hoth4]]]]].

## Summary

I continued and **finished** the Coq port of `core_refines` — the general refinement theorem that the deployed `core` RISC-V bytes implement the hex0 spec for *all* well-formed inputs. The single remaining `Admitted` (`loop_iteration`, the per-token dispatch) is now fully proved, so:

- **`Print Assumptions Hex0Coq.Refine.core_refines` → `functional_extensionality_dep` only** (no `loop_iteration`, no `admit`/`sorry`). This matches the Lean side, which was already complete.
- The whole Coq dev (`make -j`) builds clean; zero real `Admitted`/`sorry`.

### What I ported (mirroring `lean/Hex0/Refine.lean`, ~2500 lines)

Working bottom-up, committing each compiling piece (~20 commits):

1. **`loop_prefix`** — the input-read head (off 8→24).
2. **Spacing branch** — `spacing_tail`, `spacing_loopinv`, `loop_spacing`.
3. **Error infrastructure** — `error_result`, `halt_epilogue`, `bgeu_eq_taken`/`bgeu_ge_taken`, `reach_error`.
4. **Signed-branch blocks** — `li_blt/bge_nt/t`.
5. **beq fall-through chains** — `high_beq_ft`, `low_beq_ft`.
6. **Nibble parses** — `nibble_cases`, `high_parse`, `low_parse`, `high/low_parse_unknown`, `low_split`, `combine_nibbles`/`land_hilo`, `read_prefix`.
7. **Byte store** — `store_epilogue` (7-step emit), `loop_byte` (full iteration + LoopInv rebuild).
8. **Composites** — `reach64`, `reach124`.
9. **Five error classes** — `loop_trailing/split/unknown_high/unknown_low/short` + `short_result`.
10. **Comment branch** — `comment_read`, `comment_loop` (inductive scan), `loop_comment`.
11. **`loop_iteration`** — head-char dispatch assembling all branches.

### The one genuinely-new-vs-Lean piece

Because Coq's `runOn` uses *fixed* fuel (100000), I threaded an explicit fuel bound (`k ≤ 50·(chars consumed)`) through every branch lemma, so `loop_correct`'s `50·|rest|+4` total holds and the fixed-fuel run is absorbed via `runUntil_stab`. Lean used an `∃ fuel` existential and didn't need this.

Docs updated (`STATUS.md`, `RESUME.md`, the `Refine.v` header) to record that both Lean and Coq `core_refines` are now complete.

The remaining frontier for the overall project is unchanged: **task #7** (cross-check the 12-instruction ISA model against `sail-riscv-lean`/`riscv-coq` to remove "model = hardware" from the TCB).
